# Text Elements
Energy Work and Power ^gN1k7QM1

Many types of Energies:
1. Kinetic Energy
2. Gravitational Potential Energy
3. Light Energy
4. Heat Energy
5. Chemical Energy
6. Nuclear Energy
7. Elastic Energy
8. Electrostatic Energy ^3n0FX70w

Energy is NEVER created NOR destroyed, But changes from one form to another ^d4I94lSl

Petrol is Used for a Bike to be pushed ^SaqLTj6e

Gravitational Potential Energy: The energy possessed by an objects height in
a gravitational field ^OrnRjsKO

Kinetic Energy: It is the energy possessed by an object
in motion ^AV9d41Vo

Change in Kinetic Energy ^JzNUoX4p
